('COMMENT', 'random_path_up_stairs()')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '{')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '\t')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '\ttrig = getent("take_random_path","targetname");')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '\twhile(1)')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '\t{')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '\t\t\ttrig waittill("trigger",user);')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '\t\t\tuser thread take_random_path();')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '\t\t\twait(1);')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '\t}')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '\t')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '}')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', 'take_random_path()')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '{')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '\t')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '\tself endon("death");')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '\tdesired_goalpos = self.goalpos;')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '\tpaths = getnodearray("stairs_paths","targetname");')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '\t')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '\tself.goalradius = 32;')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '\tgoal = paths[randomint(paths.size)];')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '\tself setgoalnode(goal);')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '\tself waittill("goal");')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '\tat_pos = false;')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '\twhile(!at_pos)')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '\t{')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '\t\twhile(distance(self.origin,goal.origin) > 32)')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '\t\t{')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '\t\t\twait(.05);')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '\t\t}')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '\t\tnew_node = getnode(goal.target,"targetname");')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '\t\tself setgoalnode(new_node);')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '\t\twhile(distance(self.origin,new_node.origin) > 32)')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '\t\t{')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '\t\t\twait(.05);')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '\t\t}')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '\t\tat_pos = true;')
